                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Section
      2:</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Share

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Das
      Aktienkapital der Gesellschaft betr&#228;gt CHF&#160;60'944'541.20, eingeteilt
      in 304'722&#8217;706 voll liberierte Namenaktien. Jede Aktie hat einen Nennwert
      von CHF&#160;0.20.</font></div>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      share capital of the Company is CHF&#160;60'944'541.20 and is divided into
      304'722&#8217;706 fully paid registered shares. Each share has a par value of
      CHF&#160;0.20.</font></div>

      Beschluss der Generalversammlung mit der in Art. 18 dieser Statuten

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      4 <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">ter</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Das
      Aktienkapital kann sich durch Ausgabe von h&#246;chstens 16'574'894 voll zu
      liberierenden Namenaktien im Nennwert von je CHF&#160;0.20 um h&#246;chstens
      CHF 3'314'978.80 erh&#246;hen durch Ausgabe von Aktien oder Optionen an
      Mitarbeiter oder Verwaltungsr&#228;te der Gesellschaft und ihrer
      Konzerngesellschaften. Das Bezugsrecht wie auch das Vorwegzeichnungsrecht
      der Aktion&#228;re der Gesellschaft sind ausgeschlossen. Die Ausgabe von Aktien
      oder diesbez&#252;glichen Optionen an Mitarbeiter oder Verwaltungsr&#228;te erfolgt
      gem&#228;ss einem oder mehreren vom Verwaltungsrat zu erlassenden Reglementen
      und unter Ber&#252;cksichtigung der Leistungen, Funktionen,
      Verantwortungsstufen und Rentabilit&#228;tskriterien. Die Ausgabe von Aktien
      oder Bezugsrechten darauf an Mit&#173;arbeiter oder Verwaltungsr&#228;te kann zu
      einem unter dem B&#246;rsenkurs liegenden Preis, mindestens aber zum Nennwert,
      erfolgen. Bei der Ausgabe von Optionen auf Aktien hat der Aus&#252;bungspreis
      mindestens dem B&#246;rsenkurs zur Zeit der Einr&#228;umung der Optionen zu
      entsprechen.</font></div>
              </td>

      Share Capital</font></div>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      share capital may be increased in an amount not to exceed
      CHF&#160;3'314'978.80 through the issuance of up to 16'574'894 fully paid
      registered shares with a par value of CHF&#160;0.20 per share in
      connection with the issuance of new shares or options to employees or
      directors of the Company and group companies. The pre-emptive and advance
      subscription rights of the shareholders shall thereby be excluded. The
      shares or options to acquire shares shall be issued to employees pursuant
      to one or more regulations to be issued by the Board of Directors, taking
      into account performance, functions, levels of responsibility and
      profitability criteria. Shares may be issued to employees or directors at
      a price lower than the current market price quoted on the stock exchange
      on which the shares are traded, but at least at par value. In case of the
      issuance of options to purchase shares, the exercise price shall be no
      less than the prevailing stock exchange price upon grant of the
      options.</font></div>

      die Namenaktien f&#252;hrt die Gesellschaft selbst oder durch Dritte ein
      Aktienbuch. Darin werden die Eigent&#252;mer und Nutzniesser der Namenaktien
      mit Namen und Vornamen Wohnort und Adresse (bei juristischen Personen die
      Firma und der Sitz) eingetragen. Wechselt eine im Aktienbuch eingetragene
      Person ihre Adresse, so hat sie dies dem Aktienbuchf&#252;hrer mitzuteilen.
      Solange dies nicht geschehen ist, erfolgen alle brieflichen Mitteilungen
      rechtsg&#252;ltig an die bisher im Aktienbuch eingetragene
    Adresse.</font></div>

      Company shall maintain, itself or through a third party, a share register
      listing the surname and first name and address (in the case of legal
      entities, the company name and place of incorporation) of the holders and
      usufructuaries of the registered shares. A shareholder must notify the
      share registrar of any change in address. Until such notification shall
      have occurred, all written communication from the Company to shareholders

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      6</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Gesellschaft gibt Namenaktien oder Zertifikate, welche mehrere Namenaktien
      verk&#246;rpern, aus, die auf den Namen des im Aktienbuch eingetragenen
      Eigent&#252;mers ausgestellt werden.</font></div>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Certificates</font></div>

              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      6</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Company shall issue registered shares or share certificates incorporating
      a number of registered shares to the name of record owners of
      shares.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Namenaktien
      und Aktienzertifikate tragen die Unterschrift von zwei rechtsg&#252;ltig
      bevollm&#228;chtigten Zeichnungsberechtigten, wovon mindestens einer
      Verwaltungsrat der Gesellschaft sein muss. Diese Unterschriften k&#246;nnen
      Facsimile-Unterschriften sein.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Registered
      shares and share certificates shall bear the signatures of two duly
      authorized signatories of the Company, of which at least one shall be a
      member of the Board of Directors. These signatures may be facsimile
      signatures.</font></div>
              </td>

      Gesellschaft kann ausgegebene Namenaktien, die bei der Gesellschaft

      ersatzlos annullieren.</font></div>

      verurkundete Namenaktien einschliesslich daraus entspringende, nicht

      Aktienbuchf&#252;hrer.</font></div>

      registered shares, including any uncertificated rights arising thereunder,

      be notified to the share registrar to be valid.</font></div>

      verurkundete Namenaktien und die daraus entspringenden Verm&#246;gensrechte
      k&#246;nnen nur zugunsten der Finanzinstitution, bei welcher der Aktion&#228;r

      verpf&#228;ndet werden. Eine Anzeige an die Gesellschaft ist nicht

              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Ordentliche
      Generalver-sammlungen</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="3%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      9</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      ordentliche Generalversammlung findet allj&#228;hrlich innerhalb von sechs
      Monaten nach Schluss des Gesch&#228;ftsjahres statt; sp&#228;testens zwanzig Tage
      vor der Versammlung sind der Gesch&#228;ftsbericht und der Revisionsbericht mit
      dem Bericht der Konzernpr&#252;fer den Aktion&#228;ren am Gesell&#173;schaftssitz zur
      Einsicht aufzulegen. Jeder Aktion&#228;r kann verlangen, dass ihm unverz&#252;glich
      eine Ausfertigung dieser Unterlagen ohne Kostenfolge zugestellt wird. Die
      im Aktienbuch eingetragenen Aktion&#228;re werden hier&#252;ber durch schriftliche
      Mitteilung unterrichtet.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Ordinary
      Shareholders' Meetings</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="2%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      9</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Ordinary Shareholders' Meeting shall be held each year within six months
      after the close of the fiscal year of the Company; the business report and
      the Auditor's report, together with the group auditor's report, shall be
      made available for inspection by the shareholders at the place of
      incorporation of the Company no later than twenty days prior to the
      meeting. Each shareholder is entitled to request immediate delivery of a
      copy of these documents free of charge. Shareholders of record will be
      notified of this in writing.</font></div>
              </td>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">ralversamm-lungen</font></div>

              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      10</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Ausserordentliche
      Generalversammlungen finden in den vom Gesetz vorgesehenen F&#228;llen statt,
      insbesondere wenn der Verwaltungsrat es f&#252;r angezeigt erachtet oder die
      Revisionsstelle dies verlangt.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Extraordinary
      Shareholders'</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Meetings</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      10</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Extraordinary
      Shareholders' Meetings shall be held in the circumstances foreseen under
      applicable law, in particular when deemed necessary by the Board of
      Directors or if requested by the Auditors.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Ausserdem
      m&#252;ssen ausserordentliche Generalversammlungen einberufen werden auf
      Beschluss einer Generalversammlung oder wenn es ein oder mehrere Aktion&#228;re
      verlangen, welche zusammen mindestens den zehnten Teil des Aktienkapitals
      vertreten, in einer von dem- oder denselben unterzeichneten Eingabe, unter
      Anf&#252;hrung der Verhandlungsgegenst&#228;nde und der Antr&#228;ge.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Furthermore,
      Extraordinary Shareholders' Meetings shall be convened upon resolution of
      a Shareholders' Meeting or if requested by one or more shareholders who
      represent an aggregate of at least one-tenth of the share capital and who
      submit a petition signed by such shareholder(s), specifying the items for
      the agenda and the proposals.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Einberufung</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      11</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Generalversammlung wird durch den Verwaltungsrat, n&#246;tigenfalls die
      Revisionsstelle, sp&#228;testens 20 Tage vor dem Versammlungstag einberufen.
      Die Einberufung erfolgt durch einmalige Bekanntmachung im
      Publikationsorgan der Gesellschaft. F&#252;r die Einhaltung der
      Einberufungsfrist ist der Tag der Ver&#246;ffentlichung der Einberufung im
      Publikationsorgan massgeblich, wobei der Tag der Ver&#246;ffentlichung nicht
      mitzuz&#228;hlen ist. Aktion&#228;re k&#246;nnen &#252;berdies mit uneingeschriebenem Brief
      orientiert werden.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Notice
      of Shareholders' Meetings</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      11</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Notice
      of Shareholders' Meetings shall be given by the Board of Directors or, if
      necessary, by the Auditors, no later than 20 days prior to the meeting
      date. Notice of the meeting shall be given by way of an announcement
      appearing once in the official means of publication of the Company. The
      notice period shall be deemed to have been observed if notice of the
      meeting is published in the official means of publication of the Company,
      whereby the date of publication is not calculated when computing the
      period. Shareholders may in addition be informed by ordinary
      mail.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Einberufung muss die Verhandlungsgegenst&#228;nde sowie die Antr&#228;ge des
      Verwaltungsrates und der Aktion&#228;re, welche die Durchf&#252;hrung einer
      Generalversammlung oder die Traktandierung eines Verhandlungsgegenstandes
      verlangt haben, und bei Wahlgesch&#228;ften die Namen der vorgeschlagenen
      Kandidaten enthalten.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      notice of a meeting shall state the items on the agenda and the proposals
      of the Board of Directors and of the shareholders who demanded that a
      Shareholders' Meeting be held or that an item be included on the agenda
      and, in case of elections, the names of the nominated
      candidates.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Traktan-dierung</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      12</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Aktion&#228;re,
      die Aktien im Nennwert von CHF&#160;1'000'000 oder mehr vertreten, k&#246;nnen
      die Traktandierung eines Verhandlungsgegenstandes verlangen. Die
      Traktandierung muss mindestens 40 Tage vor der Versammlung schriftlich
      unter Angabe des Verhandlungsgegenstandes und der Antr&#228;ge des Aktion&#228;rs
      oder der Aktion&#228;re anbegehrt werden.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Agenda</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      12</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">One
      or more shareholders whose combined shareholdings represent an aggregate
      par value of at least CHF&#160;1,000,000 may request that an item be
      included on the agenda of a Shareholders' Meeting. Such inclusion must be
      requested in writing at least 40 days prior to the meeting and shall
      specify the agenda items and proposals of such
    shareholder(s).</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Zu
      nicht geh&#246;rig angek&#252;ndigten Verhandlungsgegenst&#228;nden k&#246;nnen keine
      Beschl&#252;sse gefasst werden. Hiervon sind jedoch der Beschluss &#252;ber den in
      einer Generalversammlung gestellten Antrag auf Einberufung einer
      ausserordentlichen Generalversammlung sowie derjenige auf Durchf&#252;hrung
      einer Sonderpr&#252;fung ausgenommen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">No
      resolutions may be passed at a Shareholders' Meeting concerning agenda
      items for which proper notice was not given. This provision shall not
      apply, however, to proposals made during a Shareholders' Meeting to
      convene an Extraordinary Shareholders' Meeting or to initiate a special
      audit.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Zur
      Stellung von Antr&#228;gen im Rahmen der Verhandlungsgegenst&#228;nde und zu
      Verhandlungen ohne Beschlussfassung bedarf es nicht der vorg&#228;ngigen
      Ank&#252;ndigung.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">No
      previous notification shall be required for proposals concerning items
      included on the agenda, and for debates as to which no vote is
      taken.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Vorsitz
      der Generalver-sammlung, Protokoll, Stimmen-z&#228;hler</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      13</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Generalversammlung findet am Sitz der Gesellschaft statt, sofern der
      Verwaltungsrat nichts anderes bestimmt. Der Pr&#228;sident des Verwaltungsrates
      oder bei dessen Verhinderung der Vizepr&#228;sident oder eine andere vom
      Verwaltungsrat bezeichnete Person f&#252;hrt den Vorsitz.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Presiding
      Officer, Minutes, Vote Counters</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      13</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Shareholders' Meeting shall be held at the place of incorporation of the
      Company, unless the Board of Directors decides otherwise. The Chairman of
      the Board or, in his absence, a Vice-Chairman or any other person
      appointed by the Board, shall take the chair.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Vorsitzende bestimmt den Protokollf&#252;hrer und die Stimmenz&#228;hler, die nicht
      Aktion&#228;re sein m&#252;ssen. Das Protokoll ist vom Vorsitzenden und vom
      Protokollf&#252;hrer zu unterzeichnen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      acting chair of the Shareholders' Meeting shall appoint the secretary and
      the vote counters of such meeting who need not be shareholders. The
      minutes of the Shareholders' Meeting shall be signed by the acting chair
      of such meeting and the secretary.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Vorsitzende hat s&#228;mtliche Leitungsbefugnisse, die f&#252;r die ordnungsgem&#228;sse
      Durchf&#252;hrung der Generalversammlung n&#246;tig sind.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      acting chair of the Shareholders' Meeting shall have all powers and
      authority necessary to ensure the orderly conduct of such
      meeting.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Vertretung
      der Aktion&#228;re</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      14</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Verwaltungsrat erl&#228;sst die Verfahrensvorschriften &#252;ber die Teilnahme und
      Vertretung an der Generalversammlung.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Proxies</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      14</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Board of Directors shall issue procedural rules regarding participation in
      and representation at the Shareholders' Meeting.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Jeder
      im Aktienbuch eingetragene Aktion&#228;r ist berechtigt, an der
      Generalversammlung und an allen dort abgehaltenen Abstimmungen
      teilzunehmen. Ein Aktion&#228;r kann sich an der Generalversammlung durch eine
      Person vertreten lassen, die nicht Aktion&#228;r sein muss.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Each
      shareholder registered in the share register is entitled to participate at
      the Shareholders' Meeting and in any vote taken. The shareholders may be
      represented by proxies who need not be
  shareholders.</font></div>

      Aktie berechtigt zu einer Stimme.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Voting

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Each
      share shall grant the right to one vote.</font></div>
              </td>

            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Beschl&#252;sse,

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      16</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Generalversammlung beschliesst und w&#228;hlt, soweit das Gesetz oder diese
      Statuten es nicht anders bestimmen, mit der absoluten Mehrheit der
      vertretenen Aktienstimmen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Resolutions,

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      16</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Unless
      otherwise required by law or stated in these Articles of Association, the
      Shareholders' Meeting shall pass resolutions and decide elections upon an
      absolute majority of the votes represented.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Abstimmungen und Wahlen erfolgen offen, es sei denn, dass die
      Generalversammlung schriftliche Abstimmung respektive Wahl beschliesst
      oder der Vorsitzende diese anordnet. Der Vorsitzende kann Abstimmungen und
      Wahlen auch mittels elektronischem Verfahren durchf&#252;hren lassen.
      Elektronische Abstimmungen und Wahlen sind schriftlichen Abstimmungen und
      Wahlen gleichgestellt.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Resolutions
      and elections shall be decided by a show of hands, unless a secret ballot
      is resolved by the Shareholders' Meeting or is ordered by the acting chair
      of such meeting. The presiding officer may also hold resolutions and
      elections in electronic form. Electronic resolutions and elections shall
      be treated in the same manner as resolutions and elections by
      ballot.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>

              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Vorsitzende kann eine offene Wahl oder Abstimmung immer durch eine
      schriftliche wiederholen lassen, sofern nach seiner Meinung Zweifel am
      Abstimmungsergebnis bestehen. In diesem Fall gilt die vorausgegangene
      offene Wahl oder Abstimmung als nicht geschehen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      chair of the Shareholders' Meeting may at any time order that an election
      or resolution decided by a show of hands be repeated through a secret
      ballot if, in his view, the results of the vote are in doubt. In this
      case, the preceding decision by a show of hands shall be deemed to have
      not occurred.</font></div>
              </td>

      bei Wahlen im ersten Wahlgang eine Wahl nicht zustande und stehen mehr als

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">In
      elections, if the first ballot fails to result in an election and more
      than one candidate is standing for election, the chair of the
      Shareholders' Meeting shall order a second ballot in which a relative

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die

      Genehmigung der Jahresrechnung sowie die Be-schlussfassung &#252;ber die
      Verwendung des Bilanzge-winnes, insbesondere die Festsetzung der

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Entlastung der Mitglieder des Verwaltungsrates;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Beschlussfassung &#252;ber die Gegenst&#228;nde, die derGeneralversammlung durch das
      Gesetz oder die</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>Statuten vorbehalten sind oder
      ihr, vorbeh&#228;ltlichArt.&#160;716a OR, durch den Verwaltungsrat
      vorgelegtwerden.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Powers
      of the Shareholders'</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Meeting</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="2%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      17</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      following powers shall be vested exclusively in the Shareholders'
      Meeting:</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;adoption
      and amendment of these Articles ofAssociation;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;election
      of the members of the Board of Directors, theAuditors, the Group Auditors
      and the specialauditors;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;approval
      of the annual report and the consolidatedfinancial
statements;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;approval
      of the annual financial statements and de-cision on the allocation of
      profits shown on thebalance sheet, in particular with regard to
      dividends;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;granting
      discharge to the members of the Board ofDirectors;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;passing
      resolutions as to all matters reserved to theauthority of the
      Shareholders' Meeting by law or underthese Articles of Association or that
      are submitted tothe Shareholders' Meeting by the Board of
      Directors,subject to art. 716a Swiss Code of
  Obligations.</font></div>
              </td>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Ein

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Einf&#252;hrung von Stimmrechtsaktien;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die

      Beschr&#228;nkung der Aus&#252;bung des Stimm-rechts und die Aufhebung einer

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;eine

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die

      Vorteilen;</font></div>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      18</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      approval of at least two-thirds of the votes represented at a
      Shareholders' Meeting shall be required for resolutions with respect

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;a

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      creation of dual-class common stock;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;restrictions

      restrictions;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;restrictions

      restrictions;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;an
      authorized or conditional increase in share</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>capital;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;an
      increase in share capital through the conversion of</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>capital surplus, through a
      contribution in kind or inexchange for an acquisition of assets, or a

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">g)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">j)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the

              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="3%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
