              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      19</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Verwaltungsrat besteht aus mindestens 7 Mitgliedern, die Aktion&#228;re sein
      oder eine juristische Person, die Aktion&#228;rin ist, vertreten
      m&#252;ssen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Number
      of Directors</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="2%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      19</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Board of Directors shall consist of no less than 7 members, all of whom
      shall be shareholders or representatives of a legal entity that is a
      shareholder.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Amtsdauer</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      20</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Verwaltungsratsmitglieder werden f&#252;r eine Amtsdauer von drei Jahren
      gew&#228;hlt. Mitglieder, deren Amtsdauer ab&#173;gelaufen ist, sind
      wiederw&#228;hlbar. Die maximale Amtszeit nicht gesch&#228;ftsf&#252;hrender Mitglieder
      des Verwaltungsrates betr&#228;gt drei Amtsperioden.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Term
      of Office</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Article 20</font></font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      members of the Board of Directors shall be elected to serve three-year
      terms. Members of the Board of Directors whose terms of office have
      expired shall be eligible for re-election. Non-executive Directors may
      only be appointed for up to three terms of office.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Jedes
      Jahr wird der Verwaltungsrat teilweise erneuert. Soweit m&#246;glich soll die
      Anzahl der wiederzuw&#228;hlenden Verwaltungsratsmitglieder jedes Jahr gleich
      gross sein und so gew&#228;hlt werden, dass sich jedes Verwaltungsratsmitglied
      nach einer Amtsdauer von drei Jahren zur Wiederwahl stellen muss. Der
      Verwaltungsrat legt die Reihenfolge der Wiederwahl fest, wobei die erste
      Amtszeit einiger Verwaltungsr&#228;te auch weniger als drei Jahre betragen
      kann. Unter einem Jahr ist dabei der Zeitabschnitt zwischen zwei
      ordentlichen Generalversammlungen zu verstehen.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: -9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Each
      year the Board of Directors shall be renewed by rotation, to the extent
      possible in equal numbers and in such manner that, after a period of three
      years, all members will have been subject to re-election. The Board of
      Directors shall establish the order of rotation, whereas the first term of
      office of some members may be less than three years. In this regard, one
      year shall mean the period between two Ordinary Shareholders'
      Meetings.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Sollte
      die Anzahl der Verwaltungsratsmitglieder verkleinert oder vergr&#246;ssert
      werden, legt der Verwaltungsrat eine neue Reihenfolge der Wiederwahl fest.
      In diesem Fall kann die Amtszeit einiger Verwaltungsr&#228;te auch weniger als
      drei Jahre betragen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">In
      the event of an increase or a decrease in the number of Directors, the
      Board of Directors shall establish a new order of rotation. It follows
      that the term of office of some members may be less than three
      years.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Wenn
      ein Verwaltungsratsmitglied vor Ablauf seiner Amtsdauer ersetzt wird,
      endet die Amtsdauer des an Stelle des ersetzten Verwaltungsratsmitgliedes
      gew&#228;hlten neuen Verwaltungsratsmitgliedes mit dem Ende der normalen
      Amtsdauer des ersetzten Verwaltungsratsmitgliedes.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">If,
      before the expiry of his or her term of office, a Director should be
      replaced for whatever reason, the term of office of the newly elected
      Directors shall expire at the end of the normal term of office of his or
      her predecessor.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Organisation
      des Verwaltungs&#173;rates, Entsch&#228;digung</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      21</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Verwaltungsrat w&#228;hlt aus seiner Mitte einen Pr&#228;sidenten und einen oder
      mehrere Vizepr&#228;sidenten. Er bestellt seinen Sekret&#228;r, welcher nicht
      Mitglied des Verwaltungsrates zu sein braucht. Der Verwaltungsrat ordnet
      im &#220;brigen unter Vorbehalt der Bestimmungen des Gesetzes und der Statuten
      seine Organisation durch ein Organisationreglement selbst.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Organization
      of the Board, Remuneration</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      21</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Board of Directors shall elect from among its members one Chairman and one
      or more Vice-Chairmen. It shall appoint a secretary who need not be a
      member of the Board. The Board of Directors shall further regulate,
      subject to applicable law and these Articles of Association, its
      organization in written organizational regulations.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Mitglieder des Verwaltungsrates haben Anspruch auf Ersatz ihrer im
      Interesse der Gesellschaft aufgewendeten Auslagen sowie auf eine ihrer
      T&#228;tigkeit und Verantwortung entsprechende Entsch&#228;digung, die der
      Verwaltungsrat auf Antrag eines Ausschusses des Verwaltungsrates
      festlegt.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      members of the Board of Directors shall be entitled to reimbursement of
      all expenses incurred in the interests of the Company, as well as
      remuneration for their services that is appropriate in view of their
      functions and responsibilities. The amount of the remuneration shall be
      fixed by the Board of Directors upon recommendation by a committee of the
      Board.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Einberufung</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="3%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      22</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Pr&#228;sident ruft den Verwaltungsrat zusammen, so oft es die Gesch&#228;fte
      erfordern, oder wenn ein Mitglied oder der Vorsitzende der Konzernleitung
      es schriftlich verlangt.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Convening
      of Meetings</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="2%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      22</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Chairman shall convene meetings of the Board of</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Directors
      if and when the need arises or whenever a member or the chief executive
      officer so requests in writing.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="12%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Beschl&#252;sse</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      23</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Zur
      Beschlussf&#228;higkeit des Verwaltungsrates ist die Anwesenheit von mindestens
      der Mehrheit seiner Mitglieder erforderlich, vorbeh&#228;ltlich besonderer
      Bestimmungen im Organisationsreglement. Kein Pr&#228;senzquorum ist
      erforderlich f&#252;r die Anpassungs- und Feststellungsbeschl&#252;sse des
      Verwaltungsrates im Zusammenhang mit Kapitalerh&#246;hungen.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Resolutions</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      23</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">In
      order to pass resolutions, at least a majority of the members of the Board
      of Directors must be present, subject to additional provisions in the
      Organizational Regulations. No attendance quorum shall be required for
      resolutions of the Board of Directors providing for the confirmation of
      capital increases or for the amendment of the Articles of Association in
      connection therewith.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="12%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Verwaltungsrat fasst seine Beschl&#252;sse mit der Mehrheit der abgegebenen
      Stimmen. Der Vorsitzende hat den Stichentscheid.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Resolutions
      of the Board of Directors shall be adopted upon a majority of the votes
      cast. In the event of a tie, the</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Chairman
      shall have the deciding vote.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
      </div>

            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="4%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="35%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Beschl&#252;sse
      k&#246;nnen im Zirkulationsverfahren (schriftlich) gefasst werden, sofern nicht
      ein Mitglied m&#252;ndliche Beratung verlangt.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Resolutions
      may be passed by way of written consent, provided that no member requests
      oral deliberation.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="10%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Befugnisse
      des Verwaltungsrates</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="4%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="35%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      24</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Verwaltungsrat hat insbesondere folgende un&#252;bertragbare und unentziehbare
      Aufgaben:</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Oberleitung der Gesellschaft und die Erteilung dern&#246;tigen
      Weisungen;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Festlegung der Organisation;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Ausgestaltung des Rechnungswesens, der</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>Finanzkontrolle sowie der
      Finanzplanung;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Ernennung und Abberufung der mit der Ge-sch&#228;ftsf&#252;hrung und der Vertretung
      betrauten Perso-</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>nen;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Oberaufsicht &#252;ber die mit der Gesch&#228;ftsf&#252;hrung</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;betrauten
      Personen, namentlich im Hinblick auf dieBefolgung der Gesetze, Statuten,
      Reglemente undWeisungen;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Erstellung des Gesch&#228;ftsberichtes sowie der Vor-bereitung der
      Generalversammlung und die Ausf&#252;h-rung ihrer Beschl&#252;sse;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">g)die
      Beschlussfassung &#252;ber nachtr&#228;gliche Leistungen von Einlagen auf nicht
      vollst&#228;ndig liberierten Aktien und daraus folgende
      Statuten&#228;nderungen;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">h)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Beschlussfassung &#252;ber die Erh&#246;hung des Aktien-kapitals, soweit diese in
      der Kompetenz desVerwaltungsrates liegt, die Fest-stellung von
      Kapitalerh&#246;hungen und die Erstattung deserforderlichen
      Kapitalerh&#246;hungsberichtes sowie dieentsprechenden
      Statuten&#228;nderungen;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Pr&#252;fung der fachlichen Voraussetzungen derbesonders bef&#228;higten
      Revisoren;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">j)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;die
      Benachrichtigung des Richters im Falle der &#220;ber-schuldung.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Specific</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Powers
      of</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">the
      Board</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      24</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Board of Directors has, in particular, the following non-delegable and
      inalienable duties:</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      ultimate direction of the business of the Companyand the issuance of the
      necessary instructions;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      determination of the organization of the Company;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      administration of accounting, financial controls andfinancial
      planning;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      appointment and removal of the persons entrustedwith management and
      representation of the Com-pany;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      ultimate supervision of the persons entrusted with</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;management
      of the Company, specifically in view oftheir compliance with law, these
      Articles of Asso-ciation, the regulations and directives;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      preparation of business reports, the preparationsfor the Shareholders'
      Meetings and the</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 28.35pt"></font>implementation of
      shareholders' resolutions;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">g)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      decision to call payments on shares that are notfully paid in, and the
      corresponding amendments tothese Articles of Association;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">h)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      adoption of resolutions concerning an increase inshare capital to the
      extent that such power is vestedin the Board of Directors of resolutions
      concerning theconfirmation of capital increases, as well asmaking the
      required report on the capital increase and corresponding amendments to
      these Articles of Association;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the
      examination of the professional qualifications ofthe qualified
      auditors;</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">j)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;notification
      of the court if liabilities exceed assets.</font></div>
              </td>

      to art. 24 of these Articles of Association, the Board of Directors may

              <td align="left" valign="top" width="35%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel
      27</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Der
      Revisionsstelle und dem Konzernpr&#252;fer, die beide von der
      Generalversammlung gew&#228;hlt werden, obliegen die ihnen vom Gesetz
      zugewiesenen Befugnisse und Pflichten. Dieselbe Person kann
      Revisionsstelle und Konzernpr&#252;fer sein</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt">&#160;</div>
              </td>

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Term,
      Powers and Duties</font></div>
              </td>

      27</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Auditors and the Group Auditors, both of which shall be elected by the
      Shareholders' Meeting, shall have the powers and duties vested in them by
      law. The duties of Auditors and Group Auditors may be performed by the
      same person.</font></div>

              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The

              <td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="35%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Die
      Amtsdauer der Revisionsstelle, des Konzernpr&#252;fers und gegebenenfalls der
      besonderen Revisionsstelle betr&#228;gt ein Jahr. Sie beginnt mit dem Tag ihrer
      Wahl und endet mit der ersten darauffolgenden ordentlichen
      Generalversammlung.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;
      </font></td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="2%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="34%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      term of office of the Auditors, the Group Auditors and (if appointed) the
      special auditors shall be one year. The term of office shall commence on
      the day of election, and shall terminate on the first Annual Shareholders'
      Meeting following their election.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1pt"><br></div>

              <td align="left" valign="top" width="35%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Artikel

      Generalversammlung kann jederzeit die Aufl&#246;sung und Liquidation der
      Gesellschaft nach Massgabe der gesetzlichen und statutarischen
      Vorschriften beschliessen.</font></div>
              </td>

      30</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Shareholders' Meeting may at any time resolve on the winding-up and
      liquidation of the Company pursuant to applicable law and the provisions
      set forth in these Articles of Association.</font></div>

      Liquidation wird durch den Verwaltungsrat durchgef&#252;hrt, sofern sie nicht

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      liquidation shall be effected by the Board of Directors, unless the
      Shareholders' Meeting shall appoint other persons as
      liquidators.</font></div>

      Gesellschaft an die Aktion&#228;re g&#252;ltig durch Publikation im Schweizerischen
      Handelsamtsblatt. Schriftliche Mitteilungen der Gesellschaft an Aktion&#228;re
      erfolgen durch gew&#246;hnlichen Brief an die im Aktienbuch zuletzt
      eingetragene Adresse des Aktion&#228;rs bzw. Zustellungsbevollm&#228;chtigten. Als
      Zustellungsbevollm&#228;chtigte gilt insbesondere die Finanzinstitution, die

      exchange regulations, all communications to the shareholders shall be
      deemed valid if published in the Swiss Official Gazette of Commerce.
      Written communications by the Company to its shareholders shall be sent by
      ordinary mail to the last address of the shareholder or authorized
